706|5d97cf|        switch lineNumbersStyle {

708|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
709|44bb33|            if lineNumber == currentLine { return "\(lineNumber)" }

300|8c7288|    var windowId: UUID {

237|70f3e8|    /// Gets the actual TreeSitter Language object for a given filename
238|f3a5e1|    /// Returns nil for plain text files (no syntax highlighting)
239|a4a35b|    private func getTreeSitterLanguage(for filename: String) -> Runestone.TreeSitterLanguage? {
240|98942b|        let ext = (filename as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
241|82335e|        let lastComponent = (filename as NSString).lastPathComponent.lowercased()
242|d6ed84|        
243|ab25ec|        // Special-case filenames without extensions
244|013551|        if lastComponent == "dockerfile" || lastComponent.hasPrefix("dockerfile.") {
245|274790|            return nil // Bash support not in package list yet
246|5f3077|        }
247|bf07fd|        if lastComponent == ".env" || lastComponent.hasPrefix(".env.") {
248|3e3e36|            return nil // Plain text
249|5f3077|        }
250|828d40|        if lastComponent == "makefile" || lastComponent == "gnumakefile" {
251|274790|            return nil // Bash support not in package list yet
252|5f3077|        }
253|4b7128|        if lastComponent == "podfile" || lastComponent == "gemfile" {
254|46c419|            return nil // Ruby support not in package list yet
255|5f3077|        }
256|0efae9|        if lastComponent == "package.json" || lastComponent == "tsconfig.json" {
257|4d9419|            return TreeSitterLanguage.json
258|5f3077|        }
259|d6ed84|        
260|f60e4e|        switch ext {
261|4c2810|        // Swift
262|1c8542|        case "swift":
263|376f7d|            return TreeSitterLanguage.swift
264|d6ed84|        
265|20fa65|        // JavaScript
266|cd5864|        case "js", "mjs", "cjs", "jsx":
267|fd14ee|            return TreeSitterLanguage.javaScript
268|d6ed84|        
269|194537|        // TypeScript - use JavaScript as fallback
270|a4d183|        case "ts", "mts", "cts", "tsx":
271|fd14ee|            return TreeSitterLanguage.javaScript
272|d6ed84|        
273|a87c1b|        // Python
274|85dfd3|        case "py", "pyw", "pyi":
275|4462da|            return TreeSitterLanguage.python
276|d6ed84|        
277|cd9e63|        // Go
278|ee50e6|        case "go":
279|44c0af|            return TreeSitterLanguage.go
280|d6ed84|        
281|fd611a|        // Rust
282|c28591|        case "rs":
283|9af65c|            return TreeSitterLanguage.rust
284|d6ed84|        
285|08c082|        // JSON
286|7aa37f|        case "json", "jsonc":
287|4d9419|            return TreeSitterLanguage.json
288|d6ed84|        
289|8aadd1|        // HTML
290|8f517a|        case "html", "htm", "xhtml":
291|d6b81f|            return TreeSitterLanguage.html
292|d6ed84|        
293|b0d395|        // CSS
294|c4efc3|        case "css", "scss":
295|27b343|            return TreeSitterLanguage.css
296|d6ed84|        
297|0fbfad|        // XML - use HTML as fallback
298|f580bd|        case "xml", "plist", "svg":
299|d6b81f|            return TreeSitterLanguage.html
300|d6ed84|

302|520b7d|        default:

304|5f3077|        }

310|6a2db5|    private func countLines(in text: String) -> Int {
311|ee3501|        guard !text.isEmpty else { return 1 }
312|c746a1|        var count = 1
313|48817a|        var index = text.startIndex
314|42136d|        while index < text.endIndex {
315|4396fc|            if text[index] == "\n" {
316|31d0c1|                count += 1
317|a7dc16|            }
318|3a0fcb|            index = text.index(after: index)
319|5f3077|        }
320|c7b6e6|        return count
321|27e597|    }

705|46d3db|    private func displayText(for lineIndex: Int) -> String {
706|5d97cf|        switch lineNumbersStyle {
707|a6eb36|        case "relative":
708|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
709|44bb33|            if lineNumber == currentLine { return "\(lineNumber)" }
710|5e67df|            return "\(abs(lineNumber - currentLine))"
711|adc83b|
712|5040ac|        case "interval":
713|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
714|bc3fe3|            return (lineNumber == 1 || lineNumber % 5 == 0) ? "\(lineNumber)" : ""
715|adc83b|
716|520b7d|        default:
717|3880c0|            return "\(lineIndex + 1)"
718|5f3077|        }
719|27e597|    }

904|c94d4f|    /// Retain security scoped access for as long as a tab referencing the URL is open.
905|80f870|    /// - Returns: `true` if access was retained (either already retained or started successfully).
906|144775|    @discardableResult
907|047478|    private func retainSecurityScopedAccess(to url: URL) -> Bool {
908|3361e8|        if let count = securityScopedAccessCounts[url] {
909|74a992|            securityScopedAccessCounts[url] = count + 1
910|40cfc4|            return true
911|5f3077|        }
912|adc83b|
913|6bae9a|        let started = url.startAccessingSecurityScopedResource()
914|eab9dd|        if started {
915|f70ee6|            securityScopedAccessCounts[url] = 1
916|40cfc4|            return true
917|5f3077|        }
918|adc83b|
919|e24e9c|        // Not all URLs are security-scoped; startAccessing may legitimately return false.
920|dc1500|        return false
921|27e597|    }
922|adc83b|
923|bb512f|    private func releaseSecurityScopedAccess(to url: URL) {
924|e6f2d9|        guard let count = securityScopedAccessCounts[url] else { return }
925|d1b9b6|        if count <= 1 {
926|a8ee0e|            securityScopedAccessCounts.removeValue(forKey: url)
927|1a1387|            url.stopAccessingSecurityScopedResource()
928|b31999|        } else {
929|385b72|            securityScopedAccessCounts[url] = count - 1
930|5f3077|        }
931|27e597|    }

934|588853|        // If already open, just activate it (and avoid re-reading / re-requesting access).
935|b525f3|        if let existingTab = tabs.first(where: { $0.url == url }) {

943|66c5ff|        // but the file is still readable. We retain access if available.

1304|8984f8|    /// Find word boundaries at a given position
1305|10f43e|    func findWordAtPosition(_ position: Int, in text: String) -> NSRange? {
1306|37ae73|        guard position >= 0 && position <= text.count else { return nil }
1307|adc83b|
1308|599630|        let nsText = text as NSString
1309|026ed8|        let wordCharacters = CharacterSet.alphanumerics.union(CharacterSet(charactersIn: "_"))
1310|adc83b|
1311|b5bfb0|        // Find start of word
1312|def66a|        var start = position
1313|aaa57c|        while start > 0 {
1314|148e5a|            let char = nsText.substring(with: NSRange(location: start - 1, length: 1))
1315|70b198|            if char.unicodeScalars.allSatisfy({ wordCharacters.contains($0) }) {
1316|0c6efe|                start -= 1
1317|f5a6eb|            } else {
1318|74cfd8|                break
1319|a7dc16|            }
1320|5f3077|        }
1321|adc83b|
1322|3d8df8|        // Find end of word
1323|f5c145|        var end = position
1324|b8851f|        while end < nsText.length {
1325|244ed1|            let char = nsText.substring(with: NSRange(location: end, length: 1))
1326|70b198|            if char.unicodeScalars.allSatisfy({ wordCharacters.contains($0) }) {
1327|fddf9a|                end += 1
1328|f5a6eb|            } else {
1329|74cfd8|                break
1330|a7dc16|            }
1331|5f3077|        }
1332|adc83b|
1333|77048a|        if start == end {
1334|1c8557|            return nil
1335|5f3077|        }
1336|adc83b|
1337|469001|        return NSRange(location: start, length: end - start)
1338|27e597|    }

>>>REPORT
## Actual app structure (entry points + scene/lifecycle)

### SwiftUI App entry point
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/App/VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift`** is the **actual entry point** (`@main`) and defines a single **`WindowGroup`** that hosts `ContentView()` and injects a single shared `EditorCore` via `.environmentObject(editorCore)` (lines **3-22**).
  - Evidence: `@main struct VSCodeiPadOSApp: App` (line **3-4**), `WindowGroup { ContentView().environmentObject(editorCore) ... }` (lines **12-22**).

### AppDelegate is used (SwiftUI lifecycle adaptor)
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/App/VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift`** uses `@UIApplicationDelegateAdaptor(AppDelegate.self)` (line **5**) so **`AppDelegate` runs**.
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/App/AppDelegate.swift`**
  - `didFinishLaunchingWithOptions` runs and registers an observer for `"WindowTitleDidChange"` (lines **15-31**).
  - `didDiscardSceneSessions` removes window state from `WindowStateManager.shared` using `session.windowId` (lines **40-49**).

### SceneDelegate situation (important)
There are **two different SceneDelegate files** in the repo:

1) **Compiled SceneDelegate (in App folder)**
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/App/SceneDelegate.swift`** implements a full `UIWindowSceneDelegate` that:
  - creates a **new `EditorCore()` per scene** (lines **31-34**),
  - hosts SwiftUI `ContentView()` via `UIHostingController` (lines **35-47**),
  - registers/restores window state via `WindowStateManager.shared` (e.g., register at line **63-64**, restore at **214-216**, save at **181-190**).
- This file is included in target sources:
  - **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS.xcodeproj/project.pbxproj`** lists `SceneDelegate.swift in Sources` (lines **588-590** in the 421-720 excerpt; and `App` group includes `2144 /* SceneDelegate.swift */` under App, lines **263-270** in the 261-420 excerpt).

2) **Legacy/duplicate SceneDelegate (top-level)**
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/SceneDelegate.swift`** is a different (older) implementation and even defines its own `WindowActivity` + `WindowStateManager` types (lines **56-89**), which would conflict with the real `Services/WindowStateManager.swift` if compiled together.
- I did **not** see this top-level `SceneDelegate.swift` referenced in the `.pbxproj` snippets read (the referenced one is under the App group). So this top-level file appears to be **dead / legacy**.

### Why the custom SceneDelegate is probably not actually *used* at runtime
- **`AppDelegate.swift` explicitly says they removed `configurationForConnecting`** to “let SwiftUI handle scenes entirely” (comment lines **36-39**).
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Info.plist`** only sets `UIApplicationSupportsMultipleScenes = true` (lines **22-26**) and does **not** include a `UISceneConfigurations` dictionary that would normally point at a `UISceneDelegateClassName`.
- Taken together, the code strongly suggests the runtime is primarily the **SwiftUI `WindowGroup` path**, and the UIKit `SceneDelegate` class is **compiled but not wired in** unless something else configures it (not present in the files read).

## ContentView structure (what the app actually shows)

### Main mode switch: “Local IDE” vs “Connected Mode”
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/ContentView.swift`**
  - Builds `mainContentView` (line **29**) which conditionally shows:
    - **`VSCodeTunnelView()`** when `tunnelManager.isConnected` (lines **106-110**),
    - otherwise shows local editor layout (`mainLayout` + overlays) (lines **111-116**).
- `VSCodeTunnelView` is a WKWebView wrapper that loads a server URL (evidence: **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/VSCodeTunnelView.swift`** lines **14-53**, **85-116**).

### Local IDE layout
- `mainLayout` is essentially VS Code-like:
  - Activity bar (`IDEActivityBar`, line **123**)
  - Sidebar (file explorer/search/git/debug depending on selectedSidebarTab, lines **125-233**)
  - Tab bar (`IDETabBar`, line **130**)
  - Editor (`IDEEditorView`, line **133**)
  - Status bar (`StatusBarView`, line **139**)
  - Bottom panel (`PanelView`) used as “terminal panel” when `showTerminal` is true (lines **143-145**).

### Editor view implementation
- `IDEEditorView` supports:
  - find/replace bar when `editorCore.showSearch` (lines **459-463**),
  - line numbers, minimap, sticky header, inlay hints overlays, autocomplete (many sections in the excerpt).
  - switches between **RunestoneEditorView** vs legacy **SyntaxHighlightingTextView** based on feature flag `FeatureFlags.useRunestoneEditor` (lines **435-437**, **490-526**).

## Wired-up features vs dead/placeholder code

### Wired up (evidence: menu commands → notifications → ContentView onReceive / EditorCore)
These menu items are actually connected to behavior in `ContentView`:
- Command Palette: `"ShowCommandPalette"` → `editorCore.showCommandPalette = true` (**ContentView.swift** line **57**; command posts in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **149**).
- Toggle Terminal panel: `"ToggleTerminal"` → `showTerminal.toggle()` (**ContentView.swift** line **58**; command posts in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **154-156**).
- Toggle Sidebar: `"ToggleSidebar"` → `editorCore.toggleSidebar()` (**ContentView.swift** line **59**; command posts in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **141-145**).
- Quick Open: `"ShowQuickOpen"` → `editorCore.showQuickOpen = true` (**ContentView.swift** line **60**; command posts in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **179-182**).
- Go To Symbol / Go To Line: wired to booleans (**ContentView.swift** lines **61-62**; commands in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **183-191**).
- New File: `"NewFile"` → `editorCore.addTab()` (**ContentView.swift** line **64**; command in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **54-57**).
- Save: `"SaveFile"` → `editorCore.saveActiveTab()` (**ContentView.swift** line **65**; command in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **74-78**).
- Close Tab: `"CloseTab"` → `editorCore.closeTab(...)` (**ContentView.swift** line **66**; command in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **86-90**).
- Find: `"ShowFind"` → `editorCore.showSearch = true` (**ContentView.swift** line **67**; command in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **102-106**).
- Zoom in/out: `"ZoomIn"/"ZoomOut"` → `editorCore.zoomIn/zoomOut()` (**ContentView.swift** lines **68-69**; commands in **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **160-168**).
- Run Without Debugging: triggers `CodeExecutionService.shared.executeCurrentFile(...)`, forces terminal open, and posts `"SwitchToOutputPanel"` (**ContentView.swift** lines **70-76**). `PanelView` listens for `"SwitchToOutputPanel"` and selects `.output` tab (**Views/Panels/PanelView.swift** lines **108-110**).
- Debugging for JS: `"StartDebugging"` triggers `DebugManager.shared.startDebugging(...)`, opens terminal, posts `"SwitchToDebugConsole"` (**ContentView.swift** lines **83-95**).

### Not wired / dead code (clear evidence in main files)
**1) Menu commands that post notifications nobody in ContentView listens to**
From `ContentView.swift`’s `.onReceive` list (lines **57-95**), these notifications are NOT handled there:
- `OpenFile` (posted by File→Open..., **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **69**) is not received → **File menu “Open...” likely does nothing**.
- `SaveAllFiles` (posted by Save All, **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **80**) is not received → **Save All likely does nothing**.
- `ShowReplace` (posted by Replace, **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** line **108-110**) is not received → **Replace menu likely does nothing** (at least from these main files).
- Selection menu: `AddCursorAbove` / `AddCursorBelow` (posted by **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **122-131**) is not received in `ContentView` → likely dead unless editor views handle it elsewhere.
- Go menu: `GoToDefinition`, `GoBack`, `GoForward` posted by **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **195-208** are not received in `ContentView` → likely dead unless handled elsewhere.
- Terminal menu: `NewTerminal` and `ClearTerminal` posted by **VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **253-261** are not received in `ContentView` → likely dead (TerminalView has its own “+ / clear / kill” UI, but the menu events aren’t connected in the main view).

**2) “New Window” is explicitly stubbed**
- File menu “New Window” has an empty action block (“Request new window via UIKit” comment only) (**VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift** lines **59-62**). So multi-window creation from the menu is currently **dead**.

**3) Debug Console switching is incomplete**
- ContentView posts `"SwitchToDebugConsole"` when starting debugging (**ContentView.swift** line **90**),
- but `PanelView` only listens for `"SwitchToOutputPanel"` (**PanelView.swift** lines **108-110**),
- and `PanelView`’s `.debugConsole` case is explicitly a placeholder text (**PanelView.swift** lines **98-103**).
So “switch to debug console” is **not wired** and the console UI is **placeholder**.

**4) JSON Tree View branch is hard-disabled**
- `IDEEditorView` contains `if false && tab.fileName.hasSuffix(".json") { JSONTreeView(...) }` (**ContentView.swift** lines **483-489**), so that code path is **dead by construction**.

**5) Commands/AppCommands.swift is intentionally empty**
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Commands/AppCommands.swift`** is only comments: “Menu commands are defined inline in VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift” (lines **2-3**) → effectively dead.

**6) Multi-window state manager exists but is only used by scene-delegate-based flow**
- **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Services/WindowStateManager.swift`** is a full persistence manager (UserDefaults save/load, capture/restore to `EditorCore`, request new window, etc.) (e.g., persistence lines **104-117**, capture **159-187**, restore **192-216**, requestNewWindow **254-281**).
- But the SwiftUI `@main` app path does not call it, and “New Window” is stubbed (above). Its main consumer is the UIKit `SceneDelegate` in the App folder.
- Given `AppDelegate` removed scene configuration (AppDelegate.swift comment **36-39**) and Info.plist has no scene configuration dictionary (Info.plist **22-26**), much of the restoration/capture pipeline appears **present but not actually hooked up** in the primary SwiftUI flow.

## Notable structural inconsistency (likely impacts multi-window)
- **`VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift`** creates **one shared** `EditorCore` at the app level (`@StateObject private var editorCore = EditorCore()`, line **6**) and injects it into every `ContentView` instance in the WindowGroup (line **13-15**).
- Meanwhile, the UIKit `SceneDelegate` path creates **a separate `EditorCore()` per window** (**App/SceneDelegate.swift** lines **31-34**).
This indicates the multi-window architecture is in flux; which behavior you get depends on whether the SceneDelegate path is active.
